    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.include.node_modules.@rbxts.playfab.out.PlayFabAuthentication
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    local Promise = require(script.Parent.Promise)
    local IPlayFabHttps = require(script.Parent.IPlayFabHttps)
    local PlayFabSettings = require(script.Parent.PlayFabSettings)
    return {
    	GetEntityToken = function(p1, p2) --[[ GetEntityToken | Line: 18 | Upvalues: Promise (copy), PlayFabSettings (copy), IPlayFabHttps (copy) ]]
    		return Promise.new(function(p1, p22) --[[ Line: 19 | Upvalues: PlayFabSettings (ref), IPlayFabHttps (ref), p2 (copy) ]]
    			if PlayFabSettings._internalSettings.entityToken then
    				v1 = PlayFabSettings._internalSettings.entityToken
    				v2 = "X-EntityToken"
    			if PlayFabSettings._internalSettings.sessionTicket then
    				v1 = PlayFabSettings._internalSettings.sessionTicket
    				v2 = "X-Authorization"
    			if PlayFabSettings.settings.devSecretKey then
    				v1 = PlayFabSettings.settings.devSecretKey
    				v2 = "X-SecretKey"
    			IPlayFabHttps.MakePlayFabApiCall("/Authentication/GetEntityToken", p2 or {}, v2, v1, p1, p22)
    		end)
    	ValidateEntityToken = function(p1, p2, p3) --[[ ValidateEntityToken | Line: 42 | Upvalues: Promise (copy), IPlayFabHttps (copy) ]]
    		return Promise.new(function(p1, p22) --[[ Line: 43 | Upvalues: p2 (copy), IPlayFabHttps (ref), p3 (copy) ]]
    				p22("Must provide an entityToken to call this method")
    			IPlayFabHttps.MakePlayFabApiCall("/Authentication/ValidateEntityToken", p3 or {}, "X-EntityToken", p2, p1, p22)
    		end)
    }

    local PlayFabSettings = require(script.Parent.PlayFabSettings)
    return {
    	AcceptTrade = function(p1, p2, p3) --[[ AcceptTrade | Line: 19 | Upvalues: Promise (copy), IPlayFabHttps (copy) ]]
